``` r
## Read in vcf and extract SNPs and variants only
library(vcfR)
```

``` r
wheat_data_gt <- as.data.frame(wheat_data@gt[,-1])
wheat_data_gt <- lapply(wheat_data_gt, as.numeric)
IDs <- NULL
IDs <- wheat_data@fix[,3]
wheat_data_gt <- as.data.frame(lapply(wheat_data_gt, unlist))
rownames(wheat_data_gt) <- IDs
wheat_data_gt <- t(wheat_data_gt)
```

``` r
yield_data <- read.csv("/scratch/pawsey1157/rtrivedi/rstudio-dir/yield_data_reduced.csv")
```

``` r
library(BGLR)

Y <- yield_data$Yield
GID <- yield_data$GID

X <- as.matrix(wheat_data_gt)

# Find matching GIDs
matching_ids <- intersect(GID, rownames(X))

# Filter yield data to retain all instances of matching GIDs
filtered_indices <- GID %in% matching_ids
Y <- Y[filtered_indices]
GID_filtered <- GID[filtered_indices]

# Match SNP data to GID_filtered, allowing duplicates
X <- X[GID_filtered, , drop = FALSE]  # Keep all matching rows

yield_data_reduced <- data.frame(GID_filtered, Y)

#write.csv(X,"SNPs_phased_reduced.csv", row.names = TRUE)
#write.csv(yield_data_reduced,"yield_data_reduced.csv", row.names = TRUE)


ETA <- list(list(X = X, model = "BL"))  # "BL" stands for Bayesian Lasso (suitable for GBLUP)
fit <- BGLR(y = Y, ETA = ETA, nIter = 5000, burnIn = 1000, verbose = TRUE)
```
